Upon detection of a privacy-related incident, our Incident Response Lead classifies the event and initiates the Data Breach Notification Workflow within our GRC platform. If the incident meets the reporting threshold, the Data Protection Officer coordinates legal, compliance, and communications leads to draft and issue controller notifications within 24 hours of breach confirmation.  Notifications include incident type, affected data categories, impact assessment, containment status, and assigned points of contact. The current notification process was independently validated during a GDPR readiness assessment in early 2025 and is tested twice annually through simulation exercises."}
